gpon
  onu profile vlan VoIP-TM tag-mode tag cvlan 2000
  onu profile vlan VoIP-MAXIS tag-mode tag cvlan 2001
  onu profile vlan TR069-TM tag-mode tag cvlan 96
  onu profile vlan TR069-MAXIS tag-mode tag cvlan 97
  profile tcont T1_3M type 1 fixed 3000
  profile tcont T1_16M type 1 fixed 16000
  profile tcont T2_2.25M type 2 assured 2250
  profile tcont T2_2M type 2 assured 2000
  profile tcont T4_100M type 4 maximum 100000
  profile tcont T2_110M type 2 assured 110000
  profile tcont T5_1000M type 5 fixed 1000 assured 30000 maximum 1000000
  profile tcont T4_1000M type 4 maximum 1000000
  profile tcont T4_1G type 4 maximum 1000000
  profile tcont T4_1.5G type 4 maximum 1500000
  profile tcont T4_2G type 4 maximum 2000000
  profile tcont T4_2.5G type 4 maximum 2500000
  profile tcont T4_3G type 4 maximum 3000000
  profile tcont T4_1.25G type 4 maximum 1200000
$
wdm-pon
  group profile Default channel-num 20 channel-space 100 up-base-freq 191300 down-base-freq 194100
$
pon-onu-mng gpon_onu-1/3/1:93
  service HSI-TM gemport 1 vlan **TMV
  service VoIP-TM gemport 2 vlan 2000
  service TR069-TM gemport 3 vlan 96
  voip protocol sip
  voip-ip ipv4 mode dhcp vlan-profile VoIP-TM host 1
  wan-ip 2 ipv4 mode dhcp vlan-profile TR069-TM host 2
  vlan port veip_1 mode trunk
  vlan port eth_0/1 mode trunk
  vlan port eth_0/2 mode trunk
  vlan port eth_0/3 mode trunk
  vlan port eth_0/4 mode trunk
  vlan port veip_1 vlan 96,2000
